<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function toggle(id) {
    var el = document.getElementById(id);
    var img = document.getElementById("arrow");
    var box = el.getAttribute("class");
    if(box == "navhide"){
        el.setAttribute("class", "navshow");
        delay(img, "/images/menu-ico_white.png", 100);
    }
    else{
        el.setAttribute("class", "navhide");
        delay(img, "/images/menu-ico.png", 100);
    }
}

function delay(elem, src, delayTime){
    window.setTimeout(function() {elem.setAttribute("src", src);}, delayTime);
}

</script>

     <div class="g-box-w center">
    <h1>NCS Index 1950 Range Colour Chart <br /><small>Natural Colour System</small></h1>
    <p>The colours depicted on the following chart are for <span class="underline">guidance only</span>.</p>
    <p>The displayed colour will depend on your monitor and browser and pearl or metallic colours cannot be shown adequately. The finished colour, therefore, may <span class="underline_bold">not</span> be as shown here. Please use the official NCS<sup>&reg;&copy;</sup> colour product for most 
	  accurate colour - available
	  <a href="https://www.e-paint.co.uk/products.asp?cat=62"><span class="underline_bold"><i>here</i></span></a>.</p>
	  <p>NCS<sup>&reg;&copy;</sup> is the registered trade name of NCS Colour 
	  AB.</p>

                        function MakeArray(n) {
	                        this.length = n;
	                        for (var i = 1; i <= n; i++) {
		                        this[i] = null;
                        }
                        return this;
                        }
                        var NumberImages024149 = 3;
                        var image024149 = 0;
